    15→ * - All API calls use CONFIG.API_BASE_URL (configurable port from .env.ports)

    36→interface Constraint {
    37→  id: string
    38→  pattern: string
    39→  message: string
    40→  severity: 'info' | 'warning' | 'error' | 'critical'
    41→  enabled: boolean
    42→  groupId?: string
    43→  suggestion?: string
    44→}
    45→
    46→interface ConstraintGroup {
    47→  id: string
    48→  name: string
    49→  description: string
    50→  icon: string
    51→  color: string
    52→  enabled: boolean
    53→}
    54→
    55→interface Violation {
    56→  id: string
    57→  constraint_id: string
    58→  message: string
    59→  severity: string
    60→  timestamp: string
    61→  tool?: string
    62→  status: string
    63→  source: string
    64→  session_id?: string
    65→  context?: string
    66→}
    67→
    68→interface ConstraintData {
    69→  groups: ConstraintGroup[]
    70→  constraints: Constraint[]
    71→  violations: Violation[]
    72→}
    73→
    74→interface ProjectInfo {
    75→  name: string
    76→  path: string
    77→  status: string
    78→  active: boolean
    79→  current: boolean
    80→  pid?: number
    81→  startTime?: number
    82→  lastHealthCheck?: number

    97→export default function ConstraintDashboard() {
    98→  const [data, setData] = useState<ConstraintData | null>(null)
    99→  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)
   100→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true)
   101→  const [expandedGroups, setExpandedGroups] = useState<string[]>([])
   102→  const [allExpanded, setAllExpanded] = useState(false)
   103→  const [projectSwitching, setProjectSwitching] = useState(false)
   104→  const [selectedProject, setSelectedProject] = useState<string>('coding') // Start with coding instead of current
   105→  const [projects, setProjects] = useState<ProjectInfo[]>([])
   106→  const [currentProject, setCurrentProject] = useState<string>('')
   107→  const [violations, setViolations] = useState<Violation[]>([])
   108→  const [violationsLoading, setViolationsLoading] = useState(false)
   109→  const [togglingConstraints, setTogglingConstraints] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
   110→  const [togglingGroups, setTogglingGroups] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set())
   111→  const [groupToggleStates, setGroupToggleStates] = useState<Record<string, boolean>>({})
   112→
   113→  // Refs for scrolling
   114→  const violationsRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
   115→  const constraintGroupsRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null)
   116→
   117→  // Force initialization if useEffect doesn't work
   118→  if (projects.length === 0 && loading && !data) {
   119→    console.log('[DEBUG] Force triggering fetchProjects - useEffect bypass')
   120→    setTimeout(() => fetchProjects(), 100)
   121→  }
   122→
   123→  // Force constraint data fetch if project is selected but no data
   124→  if (selectedProject && selectedProject !== 'current' && !data && !error) {
   125→    console.log('[DEBUG] Force triggering fetchConstraintData - selectedProject set but no data')
   126→    setTimeout(() => fetchConstraintData(), 200)
   127→  }
   128→
   129→  useEffect(() => {
   130→    console.log('[DEBUG] Initial mount - fetching projects and data')
   131→    fetchProjects()
   132→  }, [])
   133→
   134→  useEffect(() => {
   135→    console.log('[DEBUG] SelectedProject changed:', selectedProject)
   136→    if (selectedProject && selectedProject !== 'current') {
   137→      console.log('[DEBUG] Fetching constraints for project:', selectedProject)
   138→      setProjectSwitching(true)
   139→      fetchConstraintData().finally(() => setProjectSwitching(false))
   140→    } else {
   141→      console.log('[DEBUG] Skipping constraint fetch - selectedProject:', selectedProject)
   142→    }
   143→  }, [selectedProject])
   144→
   145→  // Fallback: If we're still loading after 5 seconds, try to fetch data anyway
   146→  useEffect(() => {
   147→    const fallbackTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   148→      if (loading && !data) {
   149→        console.log('[DEBUG] Fallback: Still loading after 5s, forcing data fetch')
   150→        if (selectedProject && selectedProject !== 'current') {
   151→          fetchConstraintData()
   152→        } else {
   153→          // Force set to coding project and fetch
   154→          console.log('[DEBUG] Fallback: Setting project to coding and fetching')
   155→          setSelectedProject('coding')
   156→        }
   157→      }
   158→    }, 5000)
   159→
   160→    return () => clearTimeout(fallbackTimer)
   161→  }, [loading, data, selectedProject])
   162→
   163→  useEffect(() => {
   164→    if (!selectedProject) return
   165→
   166→    const currentProject = selectedProject
   167→    const constraintInterval = setInterval(() => {
   168→      // Only refresh if we're still on the same project
   169→      if (selectedProject === currentProject) {
   170→        fetchConstraintData()
   171→      }
   172→    }, 30000) // Refresh every 30 seconds
   173→    
   174→    const projectInterval = setInterval(() => {
   175→      // Project list can refresh regardless of selected project
   176→      fetchProjects()
   177→    }, 60000) // Refresh projects every minute
   178→    
   179→    return () => {
   180→      clearInterval(constraintInterval)
   181→      clearInterval(projectInterval)
   182→    }
   183→  }, [selectedProject]) // Project-aware dependency
   184→
   185→  const fetchConstraintData = async () => {
   186→    try {
   187→      console.log('[DEBUG] fetchConstraintData starting for project:', selectedProject)
   188→      setLoading(true)
   189→      const response = await fetch(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/api/constraints?grouped=true&project=${selectedProject}`)
   190→      console.log('[DEBUG] Constraints API response status:', response.status)
   191→      if (!response.ok) {
   192→        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`)
   193→      }
   194→      const result = await response.json()
   195→      console.log('[DEBUG] Constraints API result:', result)
   196→      
   197→      // Transform the API response to match component expectations
   198→      if (result.status === 'success' && result.data) {
   199→        const transformedData = {
   200→          groups: result.data.constraints.map((groupData: {group: ConstraintGroup, constraints: Constraint[]}) => groupData.group),
   201→          constraints: result.data.constraints.flatMap((groupData: {group: ConstraintGroup, constraints: Constraint[]}) => groupData.constraints),
   202→          violations: violations // Use violations from separate fetch
   203→        }
   204→        console.log('[DEBUG] Setting transformed data:', transformedData)
   205→        setData(transformedData)
   206→        
   207→        // Initialize group toggle states ONLY if not already set (preserve manual toggles)
   208→        setGroupToggleStates(prev => {
   209→          // If previous state exists, update only new groups while preserving existing ones
   210→          const newGroupStates = { ...prev }
   211→          let hasChanges = false
   212→          
   213→          transformedData.groups.forEach((group: ConstraintGroup) => {
   214→            // Only initialize groups that don't already have a state
   215→            if (!(group.id in prev)) {
   216→              const groupConstraints = transformedData.constraints.filter((c: Constraint) => c.groupId === group.id)
   217→              newGroupStates[group.id] = groupConstraints.length > 0 && groupConstraints.every((c: Constraint) => c.enabled)
   218→              hasChanges = true
   219→            }
   220→          })
   221→          
   222→          return hasChanges ? newGroupStates : prev
   223→        })
   224→        
   225→        setError(null)
   226→      } else {
   227→        console.error('[DEBUG] Unexpected API response format:', result)
   228→        setError('Invalid API response format')
   229→        return
   230→      }
   231→      
   232→      // Also fetch violations
   233→      fetchViolationsData()
   234→    } catch (err) {
   235→      console.error('[DEBUG] Failed to fetch constraint data:', err)
   236→      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to load data')
   237→    } finally {
   238→      console.log('[DEBUG] fetchConstraintData completed')
   239→      setLoading(false)
   240→    }
   241→  }
   242→
   243→  const fetchViolationsData = async () => {
   244→    try {
   245→      setViolationsLoading(true)
   246→      console.log('[DEBUG] Fetching violations for project:', selectedProject)
   247→      const response = await fetch(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/api/violations?project=${selectedProject}`)
   248→      if (!response.ok) {
   249→        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`)
   250→      }
   251→      const result = await response.json()
   252→      console.log('[DEBUG] API response result:', result)
   253→      
   254→      if (result.status === 'success' && result.data) {
   255→        const violationsData = Array.isArray(result.data) ? result.data : []
   256→        console.log('[DEBUG] Processed violations data:', violationsData.length, 'violations')
   257→        console.log('[DEBUG] First violation:', violationsData[0])
   258→        setViolations(violationsData)
   259→        
   260→        // Update data with violations - ensure it always updates
   261→        console.log('[DEBUG] Current data object:', data)
   262→        console.log('[DEBUG] Updating data.violations with', violationsData.length, 'violations')
   263→        setData(prevData => {
   264→          if (prevData) {
   265→            const updatedData = { ...prevData, violations: violationsData }
   266→            console.log('[DEBUG] Updated data object:', updatedData)
   267→            return updatedData
   268→          } else {
   269→            // If no prevData, create new data object with violations
   270→            const newData = { groups: [], constraints: [], violations: violationsData }
   271→            console.log('[DEBUG] Created new data object:', newData)
   272→            return newData
   273→          }
   274→        })
   275→      } else {
   276→        console.log('[DEBUG] API response format issue:', result)
   277→        setViolations([])
   278→      }
   279→    } catch (err) {
   280→      console.warn('Failed to fetch violations data:', err)
   281→      setViolations([])
   282→    } finally {
   283→      setViolationsLoading(false)
   284→    }
   285→  }
   286→
   287→  const toggleConstraint = async (constraintId: string, currentEnabled: boolean) => {
   288→    try {
   289→      setTogglingConstraints(prev => new Set(prev).add(constraintId))
   290→      
   291→      const response = await fetch(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/api/constraints/${constraintId}/toggle?project=${selectedProject}`, {
   292→        method: 'POST',
   293→        headers: {
   294→          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   295→        },
   296→        body: JSON.stringify({ enabled: !currentEnabled }),
   297→      })
   298→      
   299→      if (!response.ok) {
   300→        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`)
   301→      }
   302→      
   303→      const result = await response.json()
   304→      
   305→      if (result.status === 'success') {
   306→        // Update local state immediately for responsive UI
   307→        setData(prevData => {
   308→          if (!prevData) return prevData
   309→          return {
   310→            ...prevData,
   311→            constraints: prevData.constraints.map(constraint =>
   312→              constraint.id === constraintId
   313→                ? { ...constraint, enabled: !currentEnabled }
   314→                : constraint
   315→            )
   316→          }
   317→        })
   318→        
   319→        // Project-aware refresh: only refresh if still on the same project
   320→        const currentProject = selectedProject
   321→        setTimeout(() => {
   322→          if (selectedProject === currentProject) {
   323→            fetchConstraintData()
   324→          }
   325→        }, 2000)
   326→      }
   327→    } catch (err) {
   328→      console.error('Failed to toggle constraint:', err)
   329→      // Show error feedback - could add toast notification here
   330→      alert(`Failed to toggle constraint: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error'}`)
   331→    } finally {
   332→      setTogglingConstraints(prev => {
   333→        const newSet = new Set(prev)
   334→        newSet.delete(constraintId)
   335→        return newSet
   336→      })
   337→    }
   338→  }
   339→
   340→  const toggleConstraintGroup = async (groupId: string, enableAll: boolean) => {
   341→    try {
   342→      setTogglingGroups(prev => new Set(prev).add(groupId))
   343→      
   344→      const groupConstraints = data?.constraints?.filter(c => c.groupId === groupId) || []
   345→      
   346→      // Update group toggle state immediately for UI responsiveness
   347→      setGroupToggleStates(prev => ({
   348→        ...prev,
   349→        [groupId]: enableAll
   350→      }))
   351→      
   352→      // Toggle all constraints in the group with project parameter
   353→      const togglePromises = groupConstraints.map(constraint =>
   354→        fetch(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/api/constraints/${constraint.id}/toggle?project=${selectedProject}`, {
   355→          method: 'POST',
   356→          headers: {
   357→            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
   358→          },
   359→          body: JSON.stringify({ enabled: enableAll }),
   360→        })
   361→      )
   362→      
   363→      const results = await Promise.all(togglePromises)
   364→      
   365→      // Check if all requests succeeded
   366→      const allSucceeded = results.every(response => response.ok)
   367→      
   368→      if (allSucceeded) {
   369→        // Update local state immediately
   370→        setData(prevData => {
   371→          if (!prevData) return prevData
   372→          return {
   373→            ...prevData,
   374→            constraints: prevData.constraints.map(constraint =>
   375→              constraint.groupId === groupId
   376→                ? { ...constraint, enabled: enableAll }
   377→                : constraint
   378→            )
   379→          }
   380→        })
   381→        
   382→        // Project-aware refresh: only refresh if still on the same project
   383→        const currentProject = selectedProject
   384→        setTimeout(() => {
   385→          if (selectedProject === currentProject) {
   386→            fetchConstraintData()
   387→          }
   388→        }, 2000)
   389→      } else {
   390→        // Revert group toggle state if API calls failed
   391→        setGroupToggleStates(prev => ({
   392→          ...prev,
   393→          [groupId]: !enableAll
   394→        }))
   395→        throw new Error('Some constraints failed to toggle')
   396→      }
   397→    } catch (err) {
   398→      console.error('Failed to toggle group:', err)
   399→      alert(`Failed to toggle group: ${err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error'}`)
   400→    } finally {
   401→      setTogglingGroups(prev => {
   402→        const newSet = new Set(prev)
   403→        newSet.delete(groupId)
   404→        return newSet
   405→      })
   406→    }
   407→  }
   408→
   409→  const fetchProjects = async () => {
   410→    try {
   411→      console.log('[DEBUG] Fetching projects...')
   412→      const response = await fetch(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/api/projects`)
   413→      if (!response.ok) {
   414→        throw new Error(`HTTP error! status: ${response.status}`)
   415→      }
   416→      const result = await response.json()
   417→      console.log('[DEBUG] Projects response:', result)

   419→        setProjects(result.data.projects)
   420→        setCurrentProject(result.data.currentProject)
   421→        
   422→        console.log('[DEBUG] Current selectedProject:', selectedProject, 'Current project from API:', result.data.currentProject)
   423→        // Only update selectedProject if it's still "current" - don't override user selection
   424→        if (selectedProject === 'current' && result.data.currentProject) {
   425→          console.log('[DEBUG] Setting selectedProject to:', result.data.currentProject)
   426→          setSelectedProject(result.data.currentProject)
   427→          // Since useEffect isn't working, fetch constraints directly here
   428→          console.log('[DEBUG] Force triggering fetchConstraintData after project selection')
   429→          setTimeout(() => fetchConstraintData(), 300)
   430→        } else if (selectedProject !== 'current') {
   431→          // If a project is already selected, fetch its constraints
   432→          console.log('[DEBUG] Project already selected, fetching constraints')
   433→          fetchConstraintData()
   434→        }
   435→      }
   436→    } catch (err) {
   437→      console.warn('Failed to fetch projects, using fallback', err)
   438→      // Fallback to current project only
   439→      const fallbackProject = 'Current Project'
   440→      setProjects([{
   441→        name: fallbackProject,
   442→        path: '/current',
   443→        status: 'active',
   444→        active: true,
   445→        current: true
   446→      }])
   447→      setCurrentProject(fallbackProject)
   448→      if (selectedProject === 'current') {
   449→        setSelectedProject(fallbackProject)
   450→      }
   451→    }
   452→  }

   454→  const toggleAccordionGroup = (groupId: string) => {
   455→    setExpandedGroups(prev => 
   456→      prev.includes(groupId) 
   457→        ? prev.filter(id => id !== groupId)
   458→        : [...prev, groupId]

   462→  const expandAll = () => {

   496→
   497→  const getSeverityColor = (severity: string) => {
   498→    switch (severity) {
   499→      case 'critical': return 'bg-red-500'
   500→      case 'error': return 'bg-red-400' 
   501→      case 'warning': return 'bg-yellow-400'
   502→      case 'info': return 'bg-blue-400'
   503→      default: return 'bg-gray-400'
   504→    }
   505→  }
   506→
   507→  const getSeverityIcon = (severity: string) => {
   508→    switch (severity) {
   509→      case 'critical':
   510→      case 'error': return <AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4" />
   511→      case 'warning': return <AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4" />
   512→      case 'info': return <CheckCircle className="h-4 w-4" />
   513→      default: return <Settings className="h-4 w-4" />
   514→    }

   516→
   517→  const formatTimeAgo = (timestamp: string) => {
   518→    const now = new Date()
   519→    const time = new Date(timestamp)
   520→    const diffMs = now.getTime() - time.getTime()
   521→    const diffMins = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60))
   522→    const diffHours = Math.floor(diffMins / 60)
   523→    const diffDays = Math.floor(diffHours / 24)
   524→    
   525→    if (diffDays > 0) return `${diffDays}d ago`
   526→    if (diffHours > 0) return `${diffHours}h ago`
   527→    if (diffMins > 0) return `${diffMins}m ago`
   528→    return 'Just now'
   529→  }
   530→
   531→  const getGroupStats = (groupId: string) => {
   532→    if (!data) return { total: 0, enabled: 0, violations: 0 }
   533→    
   534→    const groupConstraints = data.constraints?.filter(c => c.groupId === groupId) || []
   535→    const recentViolations = getRecentViolations(24) // Only violations from last 24 hours
   536→    const groupViolations = recentViolations.filter(v => 
   537→      groupConstraints.some(c => c.id === v.constraint_id)
   538→    )
   539→    
   540→    return {
   541→      total: groupConstraints.length,
   542→      enabled: groupConstraints.filter(c => c.enabled).length,
   543→      violations: groupViolations.length
   544→    }
   545→  }
   546→
   547→  // Helper function to get violations within specified hours
   548→  const getRecentViolations = (hours: number) => {
   549→    if (!violations.length) return []
   550→    const cutoff = subHours(new Date(), hours)
   551→    return violations.filter(v => {
   552→      try {
   553→        const violationTime = parseISO(v.timestamp)
   554→        return isAfter(violationTime, cutoff)
   555→      } catch {
   556→        return false
   557→      }
   558→    })
   559→  }
   560→
   561→  // Generate chart data for violations timeline - midnight-based with exact violation times as bars
   562→  const getViolationsChartData = () => {
   563→    const now = new Date()
   564→    
   565→    // Find next midnight ahead of us
   566→    const nextMidnight = new Date(now)
   567→    nextMidnight.setDate(nextMidnight.getDate() + 1)
   568→    nextMidnight.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0)
   569→    
   570→    // Timeline extends from next midnight back 72 hours (3 days) in 2-hour intervals (36 ticks)
   571→    const timelineStart = new Date(nextMidnight.getTime() - (72 * 60 * 60 * 1000))
   572→    
   573→    console.log('[DEBUG] Midnight-based timeline - now:', now.toISOString())
   574→    console.log('[DEBUG] Next midnight:', nextMidnight.toISOString()) 
   575→    console.log('[DEBUG] Timeline range: from', timelineStart.toISOString(), 'to', nextMidnight.toISOString())
   576→    
   577→    // Create 36 intervals of 2 hours each (72h / 2h = 36 ticks for 3 days) - ALWAYS return this structure
   578→    const intervals: ChartDataPoint[] = []
   579→    
   580→    for (let i = 0; i < 36; i++) {
   581→      const intervalTime = new Date(timelineStart.getTime() + (i * 2 * 60 * 60 * 1000))
   582→      const intervalEnd = new Date(intervalTime.getTime() + (2 * 60 * 60 * 1000))
   583→      
   584→      // Format time labels to show date and hour in "(Sep 29) 02:00" format
   585→      const timeLabel = format(intervalTime, 'HH:mm')
   586→      const dateLabel = format(intervalTime, 'MMM dd')
   587→      
   588→      // Show date around midnight transitions (22, 23, 0, 1, 2)
   589→      const hour = intervalTime.getHours()
   590→      const showDate = hour >= 22 || hour <= 2
   591→      const displayLabel = showDate ? `(${dateLabel}) ${timeLabel}` : timeLabel
   592→      
   593→      // Check if current time falls within this interval
   594→      const isCurrentInterval = now >= intervalTime && now < intervalEnd
   595→      
   596→      if (i === 0 || i === 17 || isCurrentInterval) {
   597→        console.log(`[DEBUG] Interval ${i} (${timeLabel}):`, {
   598→          intervalTime: intervalTime.toISOString(),
   599→          intervalEnd: intervalEnd.toISOString(),
   600→          now: now.toISOString(),
   601→          isCurrentInterval
   602→        })
   603→      }
   604→      
   605→      intervals.push({
   606→        time: displayLabel,
   607→        fullTime: format(intervalTime, 'MMM dd HH:mm') + ' - ' + format(intervalEnd, 'HH:mm'), 
   608→        violations: 0, // Will be populated below
   609→        timestamp: intervalTime.getTime(),
   610→        intervalTime: intervalTime.toISOString(),
   611→        actualTime: intervalTime,
   612→        isCurrentInterval
   613→      })
   614→    }
   615→    
   616→    console.log('[DEBUG] Generated', intervals.length, '2-hour intervals for 72h period')
   617→    console.log('[DEBUG] First interval:', intervals[0])
   618→    console.log('[DEBUG] Last interval:', intervals[intervals.length - 1])
   619→    
   620→    // Use violations from data object if available, fallback to violations state
   621→    const violationsToUse = (data && data.violations) ? data.violations : violations
   622→    
   623→    console.log('[DEBUG] Chart function - violations.length:', violations.length)
   624→    console.log('[DEBUG] Chart function - data.violations.length:', data?.violations?.length || 0)
   625→    console.log('[DEBUG] Chart function - using violationsToUse.length:', violationsToUse.length)
   626→    
   627→    if (!violationsToUse.length) {
   628→      console.log('[DEBUG] No violations data, returning empty intervals with zero violations')
   629→      return intervals // Return intervals with zero violations
   630→    }
   631→    
   632→    console.log('[DEBUG] Processing', violationsToUse.length, 'violations')
   633→    
   634→    // Aggregate violations into 2-hour intervals
   635→    violationsToUse.forEach(violation => {
   636→      try {
   637→        const violationTime = parseISO(violation.timestamp)
   638→        console.log('[DEBUG] Processing violation:', violation.id, 'actual time:', violationTime.toISOString())
   639→        
   640→        // Only include violations within our timeline window
   641→        if (violationTime >= timelineStart && violationTime < nextMidnight) {
   642→          // Find which 2-hour interval this violation belongs to
   643→          const intervalIndex = Math.floor((violationTime.getTime() - timelineStart.getTime()) / (2 * 60 * 60 * 1000))
   644→          
   645→          if (intervalIndex >= 0 && intervalIndex < intervals.length) {
   646→            intervals[intervalIndex].violations += 1
   647→            console.log('[DEBUG] Added violation to interval', intervalIndex, 'at', intervals[intervalIndex].time, 'total now:', intervals[intervalIndex].violations)
   648→          }
   649→        } else {
   650→          console.log('[DEBUG] Violation outside timeline window:', violationTime.toISOString())
   651→        }
   652→        
   653→      } catch (error) {
   654→        console.warn('[DEBUG] Failed to process violation timestamp:', violation.timestamp, error)
   655→      }
   656→    })
   657→    
   658→    console.log('[DEBUG] Final intervals with violations:')
   659→    intervals.forEach((interval, idx) => {
   660→      if (interval.violations > 0) {
   661→        console.log('[DEBUG] Interval', idx, ':', interval.fullTime, '- violations:', interval.violations)
   662→      }
   663→      // Force current interval to have minimal height for visibility
   664→      if (interval.isCurrentInterval && interval.violations === 0) {
   665→        console.log('[DEBUG] Current interval has no violations, adding minimal height for visibility')
   666→        interval.violations = 0.1; // Minimal height to show blue bar
   667→      }
   668→    })
   669→    
   670→    // Always return the consistent 2-hour interval structure
   671→    return intervals
   672→  }
   673→
   674→  // Get accurate statistics
   675→  const getAccurateStats = () => {
   676→    const recent24h = getRecentViolations(24)
   677→    const recent7d = getRecentViolations(7 * 24)
   678→    
   679→    const totalConstraints = data?.constraints?.length || 0
   680→    const enabledConstraints = data?.constraints?.filter(c => c.enabled).length || 0
   681→    const complianceRate = enabledConstraints > 0 ? Math.round((1 - recent24h.length / enabledConstraints) * 100) : 100
   682→    
   683→    return {
   684→      totalConstraints,
   685→      enabledConstraints,
   686→      groupCount: data?.groups?.length || 0,
   687→      recentViolations24h: recent24h.length,
   688→      recentViolations7d: recent7d.length,
   689→      complianceRate: Math.max(0, Math.min(100, complianceRate))
   690→    }
   691→  }
   692→
   693→  // Debug state values before render decisions
   694→  console.log('[DEBUG] Render decision - loading:', loading, 'data:', !!data, 'error:', error, 'selectedProject:', selectedProject, 'projects.length:', projects.length)
   695→
   696→  if (loading && !data) {
   697→    return (
   698→      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background p-6">
   699→        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
   700→          <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-64">
   701→            <div className="text-center">
   702→              <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-8 w-8 border-b-2 border-primary mx-auto"></div>
   703→              <p className="mt-4 text-muted-foreground">Loading constraint data...</p>
   704→            </div>
   705→          </div>
   706→        </div>
   707→      </div>
   708→    )
   709→  }
   710→
   711→  if (error) {
   712→    return (
   713→      <div className="min-h-screen bg-background p-6">
   714→        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto">
   715→          <Alert variant="destructive" className="max-w-md mx-auto mt-8">
   716→            <AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4" />
   717→            <AlertTitle>Connection Error</AlertTitle>
   718→            <AlertDescription>{error}</AlertDescription>
   719→          </Alert>
   720→        </div>
   721→      </div>
   722→    )
   723→  }
   724→
   725→  const stats = getAccurateStats()
   726→  const chartData = getViolationsChartData()
   727→
   728→  return (
   729→    <div className="min-h-screen bg-background p-3">
   730→      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto space-y-3">
   731→        {/* Compact Header */}
   732→        <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row lg:items-center lg:justify-between gap-2">
   733→          <div>
   734→            <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold tracking-tight">
   735→              Constraint Monitor Dashboard
   736→              {selectedProject && selectedProject !== 'current' && (
   737→                <span className="ml-2 text-lg font-medium text-primary bg-primary/10 px-2 py-0.5 rounded">
   738→                  {selectedProject}
   739→                </span>
   740→              )}
   741→            </h1>
   742→            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
   743→              Real-time constraint monitoring and compliance tracking with health monitoring ensuring dashboard (port 3030) and API server (port 3031) operations
   744→              {selectedProject && selectedProject !== 'current' && (
   745→                <span className="ml-2">
   746→                  • Monitoring <span className="font-bold text-primary">{selectedProject}</span>
   747→                  {selectedProject !== currentProject && (
   748→                    <span className="ml-1 text-xs bg-blue-100 text-blue-800 px-1 py-0.5 rounded">
   749→                      Remote
   750→                    </span>
   751→                  )}
   752→                </span>
   753→              )}
   754→            </p>
   755→          </div>
   756→          
   757→          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   758→            <Select value={selectedProject} onValueChange={setSelectedProject} disabled={projectSwitching}>
   759→              <SelectTrigger className="w-52 min-w-40 h-8">
   760→                <Folder className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
   761→                <SelectValue placeholder="Select project..." />
   762→                {projectSwitching && (
   763→                  <div className="ml-1 animate-spin rounded-full h-3 w-3 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
   764→                )}
   765→              </SelectTrigger>
   766→              <SelectContent>
   767→                {projects.map((project) => (
   768→                  <SelectItem key={project.name} value={project.name} className="min-w-0">
   769→                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 min-w-0">
   770→                      <span className="truncate">{project.name}</span>
   771→                      {project.current && (
   772→                        <span className="flex-shrink-0 text-xs bg-green-100 text-green-800 px-1 py-0.5 rounded">
   773→                          Current
   774→                        </span>
   775→                      )}
   776→                    </div>
   777→                  </SelectItem>
   778→                ))}
   779→              </SelectContent>
   780→            </Select>
   781→            
   782→            <Button
   783→              variant="outline"
   784→              size="sm"
   785→              onClick={() => window.open(`${CONFIG.API_BASE_URL}/api/health`, '_blank')}
   786→              className="h-8 px-2"
   787→            >
   788→              <Activity className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
   789→              API
   790→            </Button>
   791→          </div>
   792→        </div>
   793→
   794→        {/* Quick Stats with Navigation */}
   795→        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 lg:grid-cols-6 gap-2">
   796→          <Card className="p-3">
   797→            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Total Constraints</div>
   798→            <div className="text-lg font-semibold">{stats.totalConstraints}</div>
   799→          </Card>
   800→          <Card className="p-3">
   801→            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Enabled</div>
   802→            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-green-600">{stats.enabledConstraints}</div>
   803→          </Card>
   804→          <Card className="p-3">
   805→            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Groups</div>
   806→            <div className="text-lg font-semibold">{stats.groupCount}</div>
   807→          </Card>
   808→          <Card className="p-3 cursor-pointer hover:bg-accent" onClick={scrollToViolations}>
   809→            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Violations (24h)</div>
   810→            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-red-600">{stats.recentViolations24h}</div>
   811→          </Card>
   812→          <Card className="p-3">
   813→            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">Compliance Rate</div>
   814→            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-blue-600">{stats.complianceRate}%</div>
   815→          </Card>
   816→          <Card className="p-3 cursor-pointer hover:bg-accent" onClick={scrollToConstraintGroups}>
   817→            <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1">
   818→              <Settings className="h-3 w-3" />
   819→              Manage
   820→            </div>
   821→            <div className="text-sm font-medium text-primary">Configure</div>
   822→          </Card>
   823→        </div>
   824→
   825→        {/* Violations Timeline Section */}
   826→        <div ref={violationsRef}>
   827→          <Card className="p-4">
   828→            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
   829→              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   830→                <TrendingUp className="h-4 w-4" />
   831→                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Violations Timeline</h2>
   832→                {violationsLoading && (
   833→                  <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-4 w-4 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
   834→                )}
   835→              </div>
   836→              <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
   837→                {violations.length} total violations • Exact violation times as bars • Midnight-based 24h timeline
   838→              </div>
   839→            </div>
   840→            
   841→            <div className="h-64">
   842→              <ResponsiveContainer width="100%" height="100%">
   843→                <BarChart data={chartData} margin={{ top: 5, right: 30, left: 20, bottom: 60 }}>
   844→                  <CartesianGrid strokeDasharray="3 3" stroke="#f0f0f0" />
   845→                  <XAxis 
   846→                    dataKey="time" 
   847→                    stroke="#666"
   848→                    fontSize={10}
   849→                    angle={-45}
   850→                    textAnchor="end"
   851→                    height={80}
   852→                    interval={0}
   853→                    tick={{ fontSize: 9 }}
   854→                  />
   855→                  <YAxis 
   856→                    stroke="#666" 
   857→                    fontSize={10}
   858→                    domain={[0, 'dataMax']}
   859→                  />
   860→                  <Tooltip 
   861→                    formatter={(value: number, name: string, props: any) => {
   862→                      console.log('[DEBUG] Tooltip formatter - value:', value, 'name:', name, 'props:', props)
   863→                      return [
   864→                        `${value} violation${value !== 1 ? 's' : ''}`, 
   865→                        'Count'
   866→                      ]
   867→                    }}
   868→                    labelFormatter={(label: string, payload?: Array<any>) => {
   869→                      if (payload && payload.length > 0) {
   870→                        const data = payload[0]?.payload
   871→                        console.log('[DEBUG] Tooltip labelFormatter - payload data:', data)
   872→                        if (data?.fullTime) {
   873→                          return `Exact time: ${data.fullTime}`
   874→                        }
   875→                      }
   876→                      return `Time: ${label}`
   877→                    }}
   878→                    contentStyle={{
   879→                      backgroundColor: 'white',
   880→                      border: '1px solid #ccc',
   881→                      borderRadius: '4px',
   882→                      fontSize: '12px'
   883→                    }}
   884→                  />
   885→                  <Bar 
   886→                    dataKey="violations" 
   887→                    strokeWidth={1}
   888→                    radius={[2, 2, 0, 0]}
   889→                  >
   890→                    {chartData.map((entry, index) => {
   891→                      // Determine bar color based on current interval and violations
   892→                      let fillColor = "#e5e7eb"; // Default gray for no violations
   893→                      let strokeColor = "#d1d5db";
   894→                      
   895→                      if (entry.isCurrentInterval) {
   896→                        // Current interval - highlight with blue
   897→                        fillColor = "#3b82f6"; // Blue
   898→                        strokeColor = "#2563eb";
   899→                        console.log(`[DEBUG] Bar ${index} (${entry.time}) is CURRENT INTERVAL - applying blue color`)
   900→                      } else if (entry.violations > 0) {
   901→                        // Has violations - show in red
   902→                        fillColor = "#ef4444"; // Red
   903→                        strokeColor = "#dc2626";
   904→                      }
   905→                      
   906→                      return (
   907→                        <Cell 
   908→                          key={`cell-${index}`} 
   909→                          fill={fillColor}
   910→                          stroke={strokeColor}
   911→                        />
   912→                      );
   913→                    })}
   914→                  </Bar>
   915→                </BarChart>
   916→              </ResponsiveContainer>
   917→            </div>
   918→          </Card>
   919→        </div>
   920→
   921→        {/* Recent Violations List */}
   922→        <Card className="p-4">
   923→          <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
   924→            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   925→              <AlertTriangle className="h-4 w-4 text-red-500" />
   926→              <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Recent Violations</h2>
   927→            </div>
   928→            <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">
   929→              {getRecentViolations(24).length} in last 24h
   930→            </div>
   931→          </div>
   932→          
   933→          <div className="space-y-2 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto">
   934→            {getRecentViolations(24).length === 0 ? (
   935→              <div className="text-center py-8 text-muted-foreground">
   936→                <CheckCircle className="h-8 w-8 mx-auto mb-2 text-green-500" />
   937→                <p>No violations in the last 24 hours</p>
   938→                <p className="text-sm">Your code is compliant with all enabled constraints!</p>
   939→              </div>
   940→            ) : (
   941→              getRecentViolations(24).slice(0, 10).map((violation) => (
   942→                <div 
   943→                  key={violation.id} 
   944→                  className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 border border-border rounded-lg hover:bg-accent transition-colors"
   945→                >
   946→                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1 min-w-0">
   947→                    <div className={`flex-shrink-0 w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${getSeverityColor(violation.severity)}`} />
   948→                    <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
   949→                      <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   950→                        <code className="text-xs font-mono bg-muted px-1 py-0.5 rounded">
   951→                          {violation.constraint_id}
   952→                        </code>
   953→                        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">
   954→                          {violation.message}
   955→                        </span>
   956→                      </div>
   957→                    </div>
   958→                  </div>
   959→                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
   960→                    <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
   961→                      {formatTimeAgo(violation.timestamp)}
   962→                    </span>
   963→                    {getSeverityIcon(violation.severity)}
   964→                  </div>
   965→                </div>
   966→              ))
   967→            )}
   968→          </div>
   969→        </Card>
   970→
   971→        {/* Constraint Groups Management Section */}
   972→        <div ref={constraintGroupsRef}>
   973→          <Card className="p-4">
   974→            <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
   975→              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   976→                <Settings className="h-4 w-4" />
   977→                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold">Constraint Configuration</h2>
   978→              </div>
   979→              <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   980→                <Button 
   981→                  variant="outline" 
   982→                  size="sm" 
   983→                  onClick={toggleExpandAll}
   984→                  className="h-8 px-2"
   985→                >
   986→                  {allExpanded ? (
   987→                    <>
   988→                      <ChevronUp className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
   989→                      Collapse
   990→                    </>
   991→                  ) : (
   992→                    <>
   993→                      <ChevronDown className="h-3 w-3 mr-1" />
   994→                      Expand All
   995→                    </>
   996→                  )}
   997→                </Button>
   998→              </div>
   999→            </div>
  1000→
  1001→            <div className="space-y-3">
  1002→              {data?.groups?.map((group) => {
  1003→                const groupConstraints = data.constraints?.filter(c => c.groupId === group.id) || []
  1004→                const stats = getGroupStats(group.id)
  1005→                const isExpanded = expandedGroups.includes(group.id)
  1006→                const groupToggleState = groupToggleStates[group.id] ?? (groupConstraints.length > 0 && groupConstraints.every(c => c.enabled))
  1007→                const isToggling = togglingGroups.has(group.id)
  1008→
  1009→                return (
  1010→                  <div key={group.id} className="border border-border rounded-lg">
  1011→                    <div 
  1012→                      className="flex items-center justify-between p-3 cursor-pointer hover:bg-accent transition-colors"
  1013→                      onClick={() => toggleAccordionGroup(group.id)}
  1014→                    >
  1015→                      <div className="flex items-center gap-3 flex-1">
  1016→                        <div className="text-lg">{group.icon}</div>
  1017→                        <div className="flex-1">
  1018→                          <h3 className="font-medium">{group.name}</h3>
  1019→                          <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground">{group.description}</p>
  1020→                        </div>
  1021→                        <div className="flex items-center gap-4 text-sm">
  1022→                          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
  1023→                            <span className="text-muted-foreground">Enabled:</span>
  1024→                            <span className="font-medium">{stats.enabled}/{stats.total}</span>
  1025→                          </div>
  1026→                          <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
  1027→                            <span className="text-muted-foreground">Violations:</span>
  1028→                            <span className="font-medium text-red-600">{stats.violations}</span>
  1029→                          </div>
  1030→                          <Switch
  1031→                            checked={groupToggleState}
  1032→                            disabled={isToggling || groupConstraints.length === 0}
  1033→                            onCheckedChange={(checked) => {
  1034→                              // Prevent event bubbling to avoid triggering accordion
  1035→                              event?.stopPropagation()
  1036→                              toggleConstraintGroup(group.id, checked)
  1037→                            }}
  1038→                            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
  1039→                          />
  1040→                          {isToggling && (
  1041→                            <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-4 w-4 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
  1042→                          )}
  1043→                        </div>
  1044→                      </div>
  1045→                      <ChevronRight 
  1046→                        className={`h-4 w-4 transition-transform ${isExpanded ? 'rotate-90' : ''}`} 
  1047→                      />
  1048→                    </div>
  1049→
  1050→                    {isExpanded && (
  1051→                      <div className="border-t border-border p-3 bg-muted/20">
  1052→                        <div className="space-y-2">
  1053→                          {groupConstraints.map((constraint) => {
  1054→                            const isConstraintToggling = togglingConstraints.has(constraint.id)
  1055→                            return (
  1056→                              <div 
  1057→                                key={constraint.id} 
  1058→                                className="flex items-center justify-between p-2 bg-background rounded border border-border"
  1059→                              >
  1060→                                <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
  1061→                                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
  1062→                                    <code className="text-xs font-mono bg-muted px-1 py-0.5 rounded">
  1063→                                      {constraint.id}
  1064→                                    </code>
  1065→                                    <span className={`text-xs px-1 py-0.5 rounded ${
  1066→                                      constraint.severity === 'critical' ? 'bg-red-100 text-red-800' :
  1067→                                      constraint.severity === 'error' ? 'bg-red-50 text-red-700' :
  1068→                                      constraint.severity === 'warning' ? 'bg-yellow-100 text-yellow-800' :
  1069→                                      'bg-blue-100 text-blue-800'
  1070→                                    }`}>
  1071→                                      {constraint.severity}
  1072→                                    </span>
  1073→                                  </div>
  1074→                                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-1">
  1075→                                    {constraint.message}
  1076→                                  </p>
  1077→                                  {constraint.suggestion && (
  1078→                                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground italic">
  1079→                                      💡 {constraint.suggestion}
  1080→                                    </p>
  1081→                                  )}
  1082→                                </div>
  1083→                                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-shrink-0">
  1084→                                  <Switch
  1085→                                    checked={constraint.enabled}
  1086→                                    disabled={isConstraintToggling}
  1087→                                    onCheckedChange={() => toggleConstraint(constraint.id, constraint.enabled)}
  1088→                                  />
  1089→                                  {isConstraintToggling && (
  1090→                                    <div className="animate-spin rounded-full h-4 w-4 border-b-2 border-primary"></div>
  1091→                                  )}
  1092→                                </div>
  1093→                              </div>
  1094→                            )
  1095→                          })}
  1096→                        </div>
  1097→                      </div>
  1098→                    )}
  1099→                  </div>
  1100→                )
  1101→              })}
  1102→            </div>
  1103→          </Card>
  1104→        </div>
  1105→      </div>
  1106→    </div>
  1107→  )
  1108→}

## ✅ Dashboard Updates Complete

### 1. **Y-Axis Minimum Range**: 
- Set minimum y-axis range to 4 using `domain={[0, (dataMax: number) => Math.max(4, dataMax)]}`
- Added `allowDecimals={false}` for cleaner integer-only ticks

### 2. **Time Range Selector Buttons**:
- Added 4 shadcn-styled toggle buttons: **24h**, **5d**, **1m**, **All**
- Positioned in a rounded button group next to the chart title
- Active button is highlighted with `variant="default"`, inactive with `variant="ghost"`

### 3. **Dynamic Chart Configuration**:
- **24h**: 1-hour intervals for detailed hourly view
- **5d**: 4-hour intervals for 5-day overview  
- **1m**: 24-hour intervals (daily) for monthly view
- **All**: Dynamic intervals based on data range (2h, 6h, 24h, or 48h)

### 4. **Filtered Violations List**:
- Recent violations list now adapts to the selected time range
- Shows "X violations in last [timeRange]" or "X violations in total" for "All"
- Increased display limit from 10 to 20 violations
- Updated empty state message to reflect current selection

### 5. **Improved UX**:
- Chart automatically recalculates intervals and data based on selection
- Maintains current interval highlighting (blue bars)
- Smart time labeling that shows dates when appropriate
- Added `Calendar` icon import for potential future enhancements

The dashboard now provides much better time-based analysis capabilities with the y-axis always showing a minimum range of 4 for better visualization, and users can easily switch between different time perspectives using the intuitive button interface!

async checkConstraints(options) {\n    const { content, type, filePath } = options;\n    const violations = [];\n    const suggestions = [];\n\n    // Debug logging\n    logger.info(`Checking constraints for ${filePath}`, {\n      contentLength: content?.length,\n      totalConstraints: this.constraints.size,\n      constraintIds: Array.from(this.constraints.keys())\n    });\n\n    for    detected_at: new Date().toISOString()\n          };\n\n          violations.push(violation);\n\n          logger.info(`Violation detected: ${id}`, {\n            matches: matches.length,\n this.constraints.size;\n    const violatedConstraints = violations.length;\n    const compliance = totalConstraints > 0 ? \n      ((totalConstraints - violatedConstraints) / totalConstraints) * 10 : 10;\n\n    // Assess risk level\n    const criticalViolations = violations.filter(v => v.severity === 'critical').length;\n    const errorViolations = violations.filter(v => v.severity === 'error').length;\n    \n    let risk = 'low';\n    if (criticalViolations > 0) risk = 'critical';\n    else if (errorViolations > 2) risk = 'high';\n    else if (violations.length > 5) risk = ### Assistant

The issue is now clear: **The constraint monitoring system has all the pieces to detect violations (constraints, engine, API), but it's missing the crucial real-time file watching component that would automatically scan code changes and create violations.** 

The system currently only works when Claude explicitly calls the `check_constraints` tool, but there's no automatic monitoring of file changes. Let me create the missing file watcher service:

### Assistant

**Tool:** mcp__serena__insert_after_symbol
**Input:** ```json
{
  "name_path": "ConstraintEngine",
  "relative_path": "integrations/mcp-constraint-monitor/src/engines/constraint-engine.js",
  "body": "import fs from 'fs';\nimport path from 'path';\nimport chokidar from 'chokidar';\nimport { logger } from '../utils/logger.js';\n\nexport class FileWatcher {\n  constructor(constraintEngine, options = {}) {\n    this.constraintEngine = constraintEngine;\n    this.options = {\n      watchPath: options.watchPath || '../../..',  // Watch parent directories\n      patterns: options.patterns || ['**/*.js', '**/*.ts', '**/*.jsx', '**/*.tsx', '**/*.vue', '**/*.py', '**/*.java'],\n      ignored: options.ignored || ['**/node_modules/**', '**/.git/**', '**/dist/**', '**/build/**', '**/.next/**'],\n      debounceMs: options.debounceMs || 1000,\n      ...options\n    };\n    this.watcher = null;\n    this.processingQueue = new Map();\n    this.isRunning = false;\n  }\n\n  async start() {\n    if (this.isRunning) {\n      logger.warn('File watcher is already running');\n      return;\n    }\n\n    logger.info('Starting file watcher for constraint monitoring', {\n      watchPath: this.options.watchPath,\n      patterns: this.options.patterns,\n      ignored: this.options.ignored\n    });\n\n    try {\n      this.watcher = chokidar.watch(this.options.patterns, {\n        cwd: this.options.watchPath,\n        ignored: this.options.ignored,\n        persistent: true,\n        ignoreInitial: true,\n        followSymlinks: false,\n        depth: 10,\n        awaitWriteFinish: {\n          stabilityThreshold: 500,\n          pollInterval: 100\n        }\n      });\n\n      this.watcher\n        .on('change', (filePath) => this.handleFileChange(filePath, 'change'))\n        .on('add', (filePath) => this.handleFileChange(filePath, 'add'))\n        .on('error', (error) => logger.error('File watcher error:', error))\n        .on('ready', () => {\n          this.isRunning = true;\n          logger.info('File watcher is ready and monitoring for changes');\n        });\n\n    } catch (error) {\n      logger.error('Failed to start file watcher:', error);\n      throw error;\n    }\n  }\n\n  async stop() {\n    if (!this.isRunning) {\n      return;\n    }\n\n    logger.info('Stopping file watcher');\n    \n    if (this.watcher) {\n      await this.watcher.close();\n      this.watcher = null;\n    }\n    \n    this.processingQueue.clear();\n    this.isRunning = false;\n    \n    logger.info('File watcher stopped');\n  }\n\n  async handleFileChange(filePath, eventType) {\n    try {\n      const fullPath = path.resolve(this.options.watchPath, filePath);\n      const relativePath = path.relative(process.cwd(), fullPath);\n      \n      logger.debug(`File ${eventType}: ${relativePath}`);\n\n      // Skip if file doesn't exist (could be deleted)\n      if (!fs.existsSync(fullPath)) {\n        logger.debug(`File no longer exists, skipping: ${relativePath}`);\n        return;\n      }\n\n      // Debounce processing\n      if (this.processingQueue.has(relativePath)) {\n        clearTimeout(this.processingQueue.get(relativePath));\n      }\n\n      const timeoutId = setTimeout(async () => {\n        await this.processFile(fullPath, relativePath);\n        this.processingQueue.delete(relativePath);\n      }, this.options.debounceMs);\n\n      this.processingQueue.set(relativePath, timeoutId);\n\n    } catch (error) {\n      logger.error(`Error handling file change for ${filePath}:`, error);\n    }\n  }\n\n  async processFile(fullPath, relativePath) {\n    try {\n      logger.debug(`Processing file for constraints: ${relativePath}`);\n\n      // Read file content\n      const content = fs.readFileSync(fullPath, 'utf8');\n      \n      // Determine file type\n      const ext = path.extname(fullPath).toLowerCase();\n      const fileType = this.getFileType(ext);\n\n      // Check constraints\n      const result = await this.constraintEngine.checkConstraints({\n        content,\n        type: fileType,\n        filePath: relativePath\n      });\n\n      if (result.violations && result.violations.length > 0) {\n        logger.info(`Found ${result.violations.length} constraint violations in ${relativePath}`, {\n          violations: result.violations.map(v => ({\n            id: v.constraint_id,\n            severity: v.severity,\n            matches: v.matches\n          }))\n        });\n\n        // Store violations in database\n        await this.storeViolations(result.violations, relativePath);\n      } else {\n        logger.debug(`No constraint violations found in ${relativePath}`);\n      }\n\n    } catch (error) {\n      logger.error(`Error processing file ${relativePath}:`, error);\n    }\n  }\n\n  getFileType(extension) {\n    const typeMap = {\n      '.js': 'code',\n      '.jsx': 'code', \n      '.ts': 'code',\n      '.tsx': 'code',\n      '.vue': 'code',\n      '.py': 'code',\n      '.java': 'code',\n      '.c': 'code',\n      '.cpp': 'code',\n      '.h': 'code',\n      '.hpp': 'code',\n      '.cs': 'code',\n      '.php': 'code',\n      '.rb': 'code',\n      '.go': 'code',\n      '.rs': 'code',\n      '.swift': 'code',\n      '.kt': 'code',\n      '.scala': 'code'\n    };\n    \n    return typeMap[extension] || 'file';\n  }\n\n  async storeViolations(violations, filePath) {\n    try {\n      // Store violations in database via HTTP API\n      const response = await fetch('http://localhost:3031/api/violations', {\n        method: 'POST',\n        headers: {\n          'Content-Type': 'application/json'\n        },\n        body: JSON.stringify({\n          violations: violations.map(v => ({\n            ...v,\n            file_path: filePath,\n            detected_by: 'file-watcher',\n            session_id: 'auto-monitor'\n          }))\n        })\n      });\n\n      if (!response.ok) {\n        logger.warn(`Failed to store violations in database: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`);\n      } else {\n        logger.debug(`Successfully stored ${violations.length} violations for ${filePath}`);\n      }\n    } catch (error) {\n      logger.warn('Failed to store violations in database:', error.message);\n      // Continue processing even if database storage fails\n    }\n  }\n\n  getStatus() {\n    return {\n      isRunning: this.isRunning,\n      watchPath: this.options.watchPath,\n      patterns: this.options.patterns,\n      queueSize: this.processingQueue.size,\n      watchedFiles: this.watcher ? Object.keys(this.watcher.getWatched()).length : 0\n    };\n  }\n}"
}
```

this.app.use(express.json());\n        \n        // Redirect to professional dashboard running on Next.js\n        this.app.get('/', (req, res) => {\n registryData.projects[requestedProject].projectPath;\n                    logger.info(`Using requested project: ${requestedProject}`, { path: projectPath });\n                    return projectPath;\n                }\n                \n                // Fallback: find active project with most recent activity\n                const activeProjects = Object.entries(registryData.projects || {})\n                    .filter(([name, info]) => info.status === 'active')\n                    .sort(([,a], [,b]) => (b.lastHealthCheck || 0) - (a.lastHealthCheck || 0));\n                \n                if (activeProjects.length > 0) {\n                    const [projectName, projectInfo] = activeProjects[0];\n                    logger.info(`Using most recently active project: ${projectName}`, { path: projectInfo.projectPath });\n                    return projectInfo.projectPath;\n                }\n                \n                logger.warn('No active projects found in LSL registry, using current working directory');\n                return process.cwd();\n                \n            } catch (registryError) {\n                logger.warn('Could not read LSL registry, using determine current project path', { error: error.message });\n            return process.cwd();\n        }\n    }\n\n    async handleGetStatus(req, res) {\n        try {\n            const status = || 8.5,\n                    active_violations: status.violations || 0,\n                    trajectory: status.trajectory || 'exploring',\n                    risk_level: status.risk || 'low',\n                    interventions: status.interventions || 0,\n                    healthy: status.healthy !== false,\n                    last_updated: new Date().toISOString()\n                }\n            });\n        } catch (error) {\n            logger.error('Failed to get status', { error: error.message });\n            res.status(500).json({\n                status: 'error',\n includeGroups = req.query.grouped === 'true';\n            \n            if (includeGroups) {\n                // Return grouped constraints with metadata (project-specific)\n                const      }\n                });\n            } else {\n                // Return flat constraints list (legacy format, project-specific)\n                const constraints = this.config.getProjectConstraints(projectPath);\n                \n                res.json({\n                    status: 'success',\n                    data: constraints.map(constraint => ({\n                        id: constraint.id,\n                        groupId: constraint.group,\n                        pattern: constraint.pattern,\n                        message: constraint.message,\n                error: error.message\n            });\n        }\n    }\n\n    async handleGetViolations(req, res) {\n        try {\n            let violations = [];\n            const requestedProject = req.query.project || req.headers['x-project-name'];\n            \n            // Try to get enhanced live session violations\n            try {\n                const enhancedEndpointPath = join(__dirname, '../../../scripts/enhanced-constraint-endpoint.js');\n                const enhancedEndpoint = await import(enhancedEndpointPath);\n                \n                const              // Transform violations for dashboard display\n                violations = (history.violations || []).map(violation => ({\n                    id: violation.id,\n                    constraint_id: violation.constraint_id,\n                    message: violation.message,\n                    severity: violation.severity,\n                    timestamp: violation.timestamp,\n                    tool: violation.tool,\n                    status: 'active',\n                    source: 'live_session',\n                    session_id: violation.sessionId,\n                    context: violation.context,\n                    repository: violation.context || 'unknown' // Ensure repository field exists\n                }));\n                \n                // Filter violations by project if requested\n                if (requestedProject) {\n                    logger.info(`Filtering violations for project: ${requestedProject}`, {\n                        totalViolations: violations.length,\n                        project: requestedProject\n                    });\n                    \n                    violations = violations.filter(v => \n                        v.context === requestedProject || \n                        v.repository === requestedProject\n                    );\n                    \n                    logger.info(`Filtered violations result`, {\n                        remainingViolations: violations.length,\n                        project: requestedProject\n                    });\n                }\n                \n                // Recalculate statistics after filtering\n                const filteredCount = violations.length;\n                const severityBreakdown = violations.reduce((acc, v) => {\n                    acc[v.severity] = (acc[v.severity] || 0) + 1;\n                    return acc;\n                }, {});\n                \n                // Add live session metadata\n                const responseData = {\n                    violations: violations,\n                    live_session: {\n                        active_count: violations.filter(v => {\n                            const hourAgo = Date.now() - (60 * 60 * 1000);\n                            return new Date(v.timestamp).getTime() > hourAgo;\n                        }).length,\n                        compliance_score: this.calculateComplianceScore(violations),\n                        trends: violations.length > 0 ? 'violations_detected' : 'stable',\n                        most_recent: violations[violations.length - 1] || null\n                    },\n                    statistics: {\n                        total_count: filteredCount,\n                        severity_breakdown: severityBreakdown,\n                        project_filter: requestedProject || 'all'\n                    }\n                };\n                \n                res.json({\n                    status: 'success',\n                    data: responseData.violations,\n                    meta: {\n                        total: responseData.statistics.total_count,\n                        live_session: responseData.live_session,\n                        statistics: responseData.statistics,\n                        source: 'enhanced_live_logging',\n                        filtered_by: requestedProject || 'none'\n                    }\n                });\n                \n            } catch (enhancedError) {\n                logger.warn('Enhanced violations not available, using default', { error: enhancedError.message });\n                \n                // Fallback to empty violations\n                res.json({\n                    status: 'success',\n                    data: violations,\n                    meta: {\n                        total: 0,\n                        source: 'default',\n
